	</li><li _ngcontent-c6="" class="header__section header__color--default-gray" classname="header__section header__color--default-gray">

		</a>
	</li><li _ngcontent-c6="" class="header__section header__color--default-gray" classname="header__section header__color--default-gray">

	<div _ngcontent-c15="" innerhtml="<div id=&quot;attachment_2245&quot; class=&quot;wp-caption wp-caption-wrap alignnone&quot;> 
 <div class=&quot;article-body-image&quot;> 
  <progressive-image class=&quot;size-large wp-image-2245&quot; src=&quot;https://blogs-images.forbes.com/laurenorsini/files/2019/07/18-Kobayashi-Dragon-Maid-1200x637.jpg&quot; alt=&quot;Art from 'Miss Kobayashi's Dragon Maid,' a 2017 anime from KyoAni.&quot; data-height=&quot;637&quot; data-width=&quot;1200&quot;></progressive-image> 
 </div> 
 <div class=&quot;article-image-caption&quot;> 
  <div class=&quot;caption-container&quot; ng-class=&quot;caption_state&quot;> 
   <p class=&quot;wp-caption-text&quot;>Art from 'Miss Kobayashi's Dragon Maid,' a 2017 anime from KyoAni.</p> 
   <small class=&quot;article-photo-credit&quot;>Kyoto Animation</small> 
  </div> 
 </div> 
</div> 
<p>A week after a <a href=&quot;https://www.forbes.com/sites/olliebarder/2019/07/18/kyoto-animation-fire-claims-33-lives-and-leaves-a-nation-in-shock/#3a8fbd1580ac&quot; target=&quot;_self&quot; data-ga-track=&quot;InternalLink:https://www.forbes.com/sites/olliebarder/2019/07/18/kyoto-animation-fire-claims-33-lives-and-leaves-a-nation-in-shock/#3a8fbd1580ac&quot;>tragic fire at Kyoto Animation’s No.1 Studio</a>, which left 34 people dead, fans have reached into their wallets to show their support.</p> 
<p>Combined fundraisers including a GoFundMe from North American anime licensing company Sentai Filmworks and a direct donation link to Kyoto Animation’s bank account have raised more than $5 million for the victims since Thursday, July 18.</p> 
<p><b>See also: </b><a href=&quot;https://www.forbes.com/sites/laurenorsini/2019/07/19/the-impact-of-kyoto-animation-5-things-you-need-to-know/#1687d14460d6&quot; target=&quot;_self&quot; data-ga-track=&quot;InternalLink:https://www.forbes.com/sites/laurenorsini/2019/07/19/the-impact-of-kyoto-animation-5-things-you-need-to-know/#1687d14460d6&quot;><b data-ga-track=&quot;InternalLink:https://www.forbes.com/sites/laurenorsini/2019/07/19/the-impact-of-kyoto-animation-5-things-you-need-to-know/#1687d14460d6&quot;>The Impact Of Kyoto Animation: 5 Things You Need To Know</b></a></p> 
<p> 
 </p> 
<p>Located in Uji, Kyoto Prefecture, Japan, Kyoto Animation established itself as a pillar of the animation industry with beloved titles like international hit movie <i>A Silent Voice</i> and instant fan classics like <i><span style=&quot;font-weight: 400&quot;>K-On!</span></i><span style=&quot;font-weight: 400&quot;>, </span><i><span style=&quot;font-weight: 400&quot;>Free! Iwatobi Swim Club</span></i><span style=&quot;font-weight: 400&quot;>, and </span><i><span style=&quot;font-weight: 400&quot;>The Melancholy of Haruhi Suzumiya</span></i><span style=&quot;font-weight: 400&quot;>. It differentiates itself from most other anime studios by </span><a href=&quot;https://www.forbes.com/sites/laurenorsini/2019/07/19/the-impact-of-kyoto-animation-5-things-you-need-to-know/#1687d14460d6&quot; target=&quot;_self&quot; data-ga-track=&quot;InternalLink:https://www.forbes.com/sites/laurenorsini/2019/07/19/the-impact-of-kyoto-animation-5-things-you-need-to-know/#1687d14460d6&quot;><span style=&quot;font-weight: 400&quot; data-ga-track=&quot;InternalLink:https://www.forbes.com/sites/laurenorsini/2019/07/19/the-impact-of-kyoto-animation-5-things-you-need-to-know/#1687d14460d6&quot;>hiring animators as salaried employees</span></a>, rather than contractors paid by the frame, so animators can focus on quality over quantity.</p> 
<p>On July 18, one of the Kyoto Animation buildings was the target of a suspected arson attack that claimed 34 lives, including those of 13 men and 21 women. Thirty-four additional victims were injured. Most of the victims were <a href=&quot;https://www.theguardian.com/world/2019/jul/20/kyoto-animation-studio-fire-victims-mostly-in-their-20s-and-30s&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; rel=&quot;nofollow noopener&quot; data-ga-track=&quot;ExternalLink:https://www.theguardian.com/world/2019/jul/20/kyoto-animation-studio-fire-victims-mostly-in-their-20s-and-30s&quot;>in their 20s and 30s</a>.</p> 
<div class=&quot;vestpocket&quot; vest-pocket=&quot;&quot;></div> 
<p><b>See also: </b><a href=&quot;https://www.forbes.com/sites/olliebarder/2019/07/18/kyoto-animation-fire-claims-33-lives-and-leaves-a-nation-in-shock/#3a8fbd1580ac&quot; target=&quot;_self&quot; data-ga-track=&quot;InternalLink:https://www.forbes.com/sites/olliebarder/2019/07/18/kyoto-animation-fire-claims-33-lives-and-leaves-a-nation-in-shock/#3a8fbd1580ac&quot;><b data-ga-track=&quot;InternalLink:https://www.forbes.com/sites/olliebarder/2019/07/18/kyoto-animation-fire-claims-33-lives-and-leaves-a-nation-in-shock/#3a8fbd1580ac&quot;>Kyoto Animation Fire Claims 33 Lives And Leaves A Nation In Shock</b></a></p> 
<p>Now, surviving animators, including some who <a href=&quot;https://www.crunchyroll.com/anime-news/2019/07/26/kyoto-animation-survivors-from-studio-1-return-to-work?utm_source=community_cr&amp;amp;utm_medium=twitter&amp;amp;utm_campaign=news&amp;amp;referrer=community_cr_twitter_news&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; rel=&quot;nofollow noopener&quot; data-ga-track=&quot;ExternalLink:https://www.crunchyroll.com/anime-news/2019/07/26/kyoto-animation-survivors-from-studio-1-return-to-work?utm_source=community_cr&amp;amp;utm_medium=twitter&amp;amp;utm_campaign=news&amp;amp;referrer=community_cr_twitter_news&quot;><span style=&quot;font-weight: 400&quot; data-ga-track=&quot;ExternalLink:https://www.crunchyroll.com/anime-news/2019/07/26/kyoto-animation-survivors-from-studio-1-return-to-work?utm_source=community_cr&amp;amp;utm_medium=twitter&amp;amp;utm_campaign=news&amp;amp;referrer=community_cr_twitter_news&quot;>dove out of second-story windows</span></a><span style=&quot;font-weight: 400&quot;> to escape the flames, are </span><a href=&quot;https://www.ktv.jp/news/articles/94cbcbe4952142f988acbec47e0f3391.html&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; rel=&quot;nofollow noopener&quot; data-ga-track=&quot;ExternalLink:https://www.ktv.jp/news/articles/94cbcbe4952142f988acbec47e0f3391.html&quot;><span style=&quot;font-weight: 400&quot; data-ga-track=&quot;ExternalLink:https://www.ktv.jp/news/articles/94cbcbe4952142f988acbec47e0f3391.html&quot;>returning to work</span></a><span style=&quot;font-weight: 400&quot;> to attempt the uphill climb of rebuilding the studio’s legacy. But thanks to monetary support, KyoAni, as the studio is called by fans, won’t be doing it alone.&amp;nbsp;</span></p> 
<p><span style=&quot;font-weight: 400&quot;>Daisuke Okeda, the lawyer representing Kyoto Animation, </span><a href=&quot;https://twitter.com/DaisukeP/status/1154565063723773952&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; rel=&quot;nofollow noopener&quot; data-ga-track=&quot;ExternalLink:https://twitter.com/DaisukeP/status/1154565063723773952&quot;><span style=&quot;font-weight: 400&quot; data-ga-track=&quot;ExternalLink:https://twitter.com/DaisukeP/status/1154565063723773952&quot;>tweeted</span></a><span style=&quot;font-weight: 400&quot;> that within 48 hours of posting the direct deposit information to donate to the studio’s bank account, </span><a href=&quot;https://twitter.com/DaisukeP/status/1154565063723773952&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; rel=&quot;nofollow noopener&quot; data-ga-track=&quot;ExternalLink:https://twitter.com/DaisukeP/status/1154565063723773952&quot;><span style=&quot;font-weight: 400&quot; data-ga-track=&quot;ExternalLink:https://twitter.com/DaisukeP/status/1154565063723773952&quot;>it had raised 401,255,554 yen</span></a> or about $3,693,176.</p> 
<p>Meanwhile, Sentai Filmworks, which posted its GoFundMe the night of the fire, has <a href=&quot;https://www.gofundme.com/f/help-kyoani-heal&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; rel=&quot;nofollow noopener&quot; data-ga-track=&quot;ExternalLink:https://www.gofundme.com/f/help-kyoani-heal&quot;>raised more than $2 million</a> for the studio. In response to fans’ questions, the company <a href=&quot;https://twitter.com/SentaiFilmworks/status/1154393937098039297&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; rel=&quot;nofollow noopener&quot; data-ga-track=&quot;ExternalLink:https://twitter.com/SentaiFilmworks/status/1154393937098039297&quot;>released a statement Thursday</a> that it is “working with KyoAni’s appointed representative” to ensure the funds “reach the KyoAni victims and their families in a direct and meaningful way.”</p> 
<p>Other organizations, including a collaboration between Yahoo! Japan and JAniCA (Japanese Animation Creators Association), are also collecting funds for the victims. As of Friday, July 26, this fundraiser <a href=&quot;https://donation.yahoo.co.jp/detail/5234001/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; rel=&quot;nofollow noopener&quot; data-ga-track=&quot;ExternalLink:https://donation.yahoo.co.jp/detail/5234001/&quot;>has netted 3,409,930 yen</a> or about $31,381.59.</p> 
<p>Right now, the most straightforward way for fans to send monetary support to Kyoto Animation is to send a direct donation using the <a href=&quot;http://www.kyotoanimation.co.jp/information/?id=3075&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot; rel=&quot;nofollow noopener&quot; data-ga-track=&quot;ExternalLink:http://www.kyotoanimation.co.jp/information/?id=3075&quot;>bank information the company has released itself</a>, including a SWIFT code for international transfers. The bank account holder is Hideaki Hatta, the president of Kyoto Animation.</p> 
<p>The information for donating is listed below.</p> 
<p>BANK NAME : THE KYOTO SHINKIN BANK</p> 
<p>SWIFT : KYSBJPJZ</p> 
<p>BRANCH NAME : MINAMI MOMOYAMA BRANCH</p> 
<p>BRANCH NUMBER : 048</p> 
<p>ADDRESS : 16-50, YOSAI, MOMOYAMA-CHO, HUSHIMI-KU, KYOTO-SHI, KYOTO-HU, 612-8016 , JAPAN</p> 
<p>ACCOUNT NUMBER : 0002890</p> 
<p>ACCOUNT HOLDER : KYOTO ANIMATION CO.,LTD., REPRESENTATIVE DIRECTOR, HATTA HIDEAKI</p>"><div id="attachment_2245" class="wp-caption wp-caption-wrap alignnone"> 
 <div class="article-body-image"> 
  <progressive-image class="size-large wp-image-2245" src="https://blogs-images.forbes.com/laurenorsini/files/2019/07/18-Kobayashi-Dragon-Maid-1200x637.jpg" alt="Art from 'Miss Kobayashi's Dragon Maid,' a 2017 anime from KyoAni." data-height="637" data-width="1200"></progressive-image> 
 </div> 
 <div class="article-image-caption"> 
  <div class="caption-container" ng-class="caption_state"> 
   <p class="wp-caption-text">Art from 'Miss Kobayashi's Dragon Maid,' a 2017 anime from KyoAni.</p> 
   <small class="article-photo-credit">Kyoto Animation</small> 
  </div> 
 </div> 
</div> 
<p class="speakable-paragraph">A week after a <a href="https://www.forbes.com/sites/olliebarder/2019/07/18/kyoto-animation-fire-claims-33-lives-and-leaves-a-nation-in-shock/#3a8fbd1580ac" target="_self" data-ga-track="InternalLink:https://www.forbes.com/sites/olliebarder/2019/07/18/kyoto-animation-fire-claims-33-lives-and-leaves-a-nation-in-shock/#3a8fbd1580ac">tragic fire at Kyoto Animation’s No.1 Studio</a>, which left 34 people dead, fans have reached into their wallets to show their support.</p> 
<p>Combined fundraisers including a GoFundMe from North American anime licensing company Sentai Filmworks and a direct donation link to Kyoto Animation’s bank account have raised more than $5 million for the victims since Thursday, July 18.</p> 
<p><b>See also: </b><a href="https://www.forbes.com/sites/laurenorsini/2019/07/19/the-impact-of-kyoto-animation-5-things-you-need-to-know/#1687d14460d6" target="_self" data-ga-track="InternalLink:https://www.forbes.com/sites/laurenorsini/2019/07/19/the-impact-of-kyoto-animation-5-things-you-need-to-know/#1687d14460d6"><b data-ga-track="InternalLink:https://www.forbes.com/sites/laurenorsini/2019/07/19/the-impact-of-kyoto-animation-5-things-you-need-to-know/#1687d14460d6">The Impact Of Kyoto Animation: 5 Things You Need To Know</b></a></p> 
<p> 
 </p> 
<p>Located in Uji, Kyoto Prefecture, Japan, Kyoto Animation established itself as a pillar of the animation industry with beloved titles like international hit movie <i>A Silent Voice</i> and instant fan classics like <i><span style="font-weight: 400">K-On!</span></i><span style="font-weight: 400">, </span><i><span style="font-weight: 400">Free! Iwatobi Swim Club</span></i><span style="font-weight: 400">, and </span><i><span style="font-weight: 400">The Melancholy of Haruhi Suzumiya</span></i><span style="font-weight: 400">. It differentiates itself from most other anime studios by </span><a href="https://www.forbes.com/sites/laurenorsini/2019/07/19/the-impact-of-kyoto-animation-5-things-you-need-to-know/#1687d14460d6" target="_self" data-ga-track="InternalLink:https://www.forbes.com/sites/laurenorsini/2019/07/19/the-impact-of-kyoto-animation-5-things-you-need-to-know/#1687d14460d6"><span style="font-weight: 400" data-ga-track="InternalLink:https://www.forbes.com/sites/laurenorsini/2019/07/19/the-impact-of-kyoto-animation-5-things-you-need-to-know/#1687d14460d6">hiring animators as salaried employees</span></a>, rather than contractors paid by the frame, so animators can focus on quality over quantity.</p> 
<p>On July 18, one of the Kyoto Animation buildings was the target of a suspected arson attack that claimed 34 lives, including those of 13 men and 21 women. Thirty-four additional victims were injured. Most of the victims were <a href="https://www.theguardian.com/world/2019/jul/20/kyoto-animation-studio-fire-victims-mostly-in-their-20s-and-30s" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener" data-ga-track="ExternalLink:https://www.theguardian.com/world/2019/jul/20/kyoto-animation-studio-fire-victims-mostly-in-their-20s-and-30s">in their 20s and 30s</a>.</p> 
<div class="vestpocket" vest-pocket=""></div> 
<p><b>See also: </b><a href="https://www.forbes.com/sites/olliebarder/2019/07/18/kyoto-animation-fire-claims-33-lives-and-leaves-a-nation-in-shock/#3a8fbd1580ac" target="_self" data-ga-track="InternalLink:https://www.forbes.com/sites/olliebarder/2019/07/18/kyoto-animation-fire-claims-33-lives-and-leaves-a-nation-in-shock/#3a8fbd1580ac"><b data-ga-track="InternalLink:https://www.forbes.com/sites/olliebarder/2019/07/18/kyoto-animation-fire-claims-33-lives-and-leaves-a-nation-in-shock/#3a8fbd1580ac">Kyoto Animation Fire Claims 33 Lives And Leaves A Nation In Shock</b></a></p> 
<p>Now, surviving animators, including some who <a href="https://www.crunchyroll.com/anime-news/2019/07/26/kyoto-animation-survivors-from-studio-1-return-to-work?utm_source=community_cr&amp;utm_medium=twitter&amp;utm_campaign=news&amp;referrer=community_cr_twitter_news" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener" data-ga-track="ExternalLink:https://www.crunchyroll.com/anime-news/2019/07/26/kyoto-animation-survivors-from-studio-1-return-to-work?utm_source=community_cr&amp;utm_medium=twitter&amp;utm_campaign=news&amp;referrer=community_cr_twitter_news"><span style="font-weight: 400" data-ga-track="ExternalLink:https://www.crunchyroll.com/anime-news/2019/07/26/kyoto-animation-survivors-from-studio-1-return-to-work?utm_source=community_cr&amp;utm_medium=twitter&amp;utm_campaign=news&amp;referrer=community_cr_twitter_news">dove out of second-story windows</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400"> to escape the flames, are </span><a href="https://www.ktv.jp/news/articles/94cbcbe4952142f988acbec47e0f3391.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener" data-ga-track="ExternalLink:https://www.ktv.jp/news/articles/94cbcbe4952142f988acbec47e0f3391.html"><span style="font-weight: 400" data-ga-track="ExternalLink:https://www.ktv.jp/news/articles/94cbcbe4952142f988acbec47e0f3391.html">returning to work</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400"> to attempt the uphill climb of rebuilding the studio’s legacy. But thanks to monetary support, KyoAni, as the studio is called by fans, won’t be doing it alone.&nbsp;</span></p> 
<p><span style="font-weight: 400">Daisuke Okeda, the lawyer representing Kyoto Animation, </span><a href="https://twitter.com/DaisukeP/status/1154565063723773952" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener" data-ga-track="ExternalLink:https://twitter.com/DaisukeP/status/1154565063723773952"><span style="font-weight: 400" data-ga-track="ExternalLink:https://twitter.com/DaisukeP/status/1154565063723773952">tweeted</span></a><span style="font-weight: 400"> that within 48 hours of posting the direct deposit information to donate to the studio’s bank account, </span><a href="https://twitter.com/DaisukeP/status/1154565063723773952" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener" data-ga-track="ExternalLink:https://twitter.com/DaisukeP/status/1154565063723773952"><span style="font-weight: 400" data-ga-track="ExternalLink:https://twitter.com/DaisukeP/status/1154565063723773952">it had raised 401,255,554 yen</span></a> or about $3,693,176.</p> 
<p>Meanwhile, Sentai Filmworks, which posted its GoFundMe the night of the fire, has <a href="https://www.gofundme.com/f/help-kyoani-heal" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener" data-ga-track="ExternalLink:https://www.gofundme.com/f/help-kyoani-heal">raised more than $2 million</a> for the studio. In response to fans’ questions, the company <a href="https://twitter.com/SentaiFilmworks/status/1154393937098039297" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener" data-ga-track="ExternalLink:https://twitter.com/SentaiFilmworks/status/1154393937098039297">released a statement Thursday</a> that it is “working with KyoAni’s appointed representative” to ensure the funds “reach the KyoAni victims and their families in a direct and meaningful way.”</p> 
<p>Other organizations, including a collaboration between Yahoo! Japan and JAniCA (Japanese Animation Creators Association), are also collecting funds for the victims. As of Friday, July 26, this fundraiser <a href="https://donation.yahoo.co.jp/detail/5234001/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener" data-ga-track="ExternalLink:https://donation.yahoo.co.jp/detail/5234001/">has netted 3,409,930 yen</a> or about $31,381.59.</p> 
<p>Right now, the most straightforward way for fans to send monetary support to Kyoto Animation is to send a direct donation using the <a href="http://www.kyotoanimation.co.jp/information/?id=3075" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener" data-ga-track="ExternalLink:http://www.kyotoanimation.co.jp/information/?id=3075">bank information the company has released itself</a>, including a SWIFT code for international transfers. The bank account holder is Hideaki Hatta, the president of Kyoto Animation.</p> 
<p>The information for donating is listed below.</p> 
<p>BANK NAME : THE KYOTO SHINKIN BANK</p> 
<p>SWIFT : KYSBJPJZ</p> 
<p>BRANCH NAME : MINAMI MOMOYAMA BRANCH</p> 
<p>BRANCH NUMBER : 048</p> 
<p>ADDRESS : 16-50, YOSAI, MOMOYAMA-CHO, HUSHIMI-KU, KYOTO-SHI, KYOTO-HU, 612-8016 , JAPAN</p> 
<p>ACCOUNT NUMBER : 0002890</p> 
<p>ACCOUNT HOLDER : KYOTO ANIMATION CO.,LTD., REPRESENTATIVE DIRECTOR, HATTA HIDEAKI</p></div>
</div>

href=\&q;https://www.forbes.com/sites/olliebarder/2019/07/18/kyoto-animation-fire-claims-33-lives-and-leaves-a-nation-in-shock/#3a8fbd1580ac\&q;&g;tragic fire at Kyoto Animation&a;rsquo;s No.1 Studio&l;/a&g;, which left 34 people dead, fans have reached into their wallets to show their support.\r\n\r\nCombined fundraisers including a GoFundMe from North American anime licensing company Sentai Filmworks and a direct donation link to Kyoto Animation&a;rsquo;s bank account have raised more than $5 million for the victims since Thursday, July 18.\r\n\r\n&l;b&g;See also: &l;/b&g;&l;a href=\&q;https://www.forbes.com/sites/laurenorsini/2019/07/19/the-impact-of-kyoto-animation-5-things-you-need-to-know/#1687d14460d6\&q;&g;&l;b&g;The Impact Of Kyoto Animation: 5 Things You Need To Know&l;/b&g;&l;/a&g;\r\n\r\nLocated in Uji, Kyoto Prefecture, Japan, Kyoto Animation established itself as a pillar of the animation industry with beloved titles like international hit movie &l;i&g;A Silent Voice&l;/i&g; and instant fan classics like &l;i&g;&l;span style=\&q;font-weight: 400\&q;&g;K-On!&l;/span&g;&l;/i&g;&l;span style=\&q;font-weight: 400\&q;&g;, &l;/span&g;&l;i&g;&l;span style=\&q;font-weight: 400\&q;&g;Free! Iwatobi Swim Club&l;/span&g;&l;/i&g;&l;span style=\&q;font-weight: 400\&q;&g;, and &l;/span&g;&l;i&g;&l;span style=\&q;font-weight: 400\&q;&g;The Melancholy of Haruhi Suzumiya&l;/span&g;&l;/i&g;&l;span style=\&q;font-weight: 400\&q;&g;. It differentiates itself from most other anime studios by &l;/span&g;&l;a href=\&q;https://www.forbes.com/sites/laurenorsini/2019/07/19/the-impact-of-kyoto-animation-5-things-you-need-to-know/#1687d14460d6\&q;&g;&l;span style=\&q;font-weight: 400\&q;&g;hiring animators as salaried employees&l;/span&g;&l;/a&g;, rather than contractors paid by the frame, so animators can focus on quality over quantity.\r\n\r\nOn July 18, one of the Kyoto Animation buildings was the target of a suspected arson attack that claimed 34 lives, including those of 13 men and 21 women. Thirty-four additional victims were injured. Most of the victims were &l;a href=\&q;https://www.theguardian.com/world/2019/jul/20/kyoto-animation-studio-fire-victims-mostly-in-their-20s-and-30s\&q; target=\&q;_blank\&q;&g;in their 20s and 30s&l;/a&g;.\r\n\r\n&l;b&g;See also: &l;/b&g;&l;a href=\&q;https://www.forbes.com/sites/olliebarder/2019/07/18/kyoto-animation-fire-claims-33-lives-and-leaves-a-nation-in-shock/#3a8fbd1580ac\&q;&g;&l;b&g;Kyoto Animation Fire Claims 33 Lives And Leaves A Nation In Shock&l;/b&g;&l;/a&g;\r\n\r\nNow, surviving animators, including some who &l;a href=\&q;https://www.crunchyroll.com/anime-news/2019/07/26/kyoto-animation-survivors-from-studio-1-return-to-work?utm_source=community_cr&a;amp;utm_medium=twitter&a;amp;utm_campaign=news&a;amp;referrer=community_cr_twitter_news\&q; target=\&q;_blank\&q;&g;&l;span style=\&q;font-weight: 400\&q;&g;dove out of second-story windows&l;/span&g;&l;/a&g;&l;span style=\&q;font-weight: 400\&q;&g; to escape the flames, are &l;/span&g;&l;a href=\&q;https://www.ktv.jp/news/articles/94cbcbe4952142f988acbec47e0f3391.html\&q; target=\&q;_blank\&q;&g;&l;span style=\&q;font-weight: 400\&q;&g;returning to work&l;/span&g;&l;/a&g;&l;span style=\&q;font-weight: 400\&q;&g; to attempt the uphill climb of rebuilding the studio&a;rsquo;s legacy. But thanks to monetary support, KyoAni, as the studio is called by fans, won&a;rsquo;t be doing it alone.&a;nbsp;&l;/span&g;\r\n\r\n&l;span style=\&q;font-weight: 400\&q;&g;Daisuke Okeda, the lawyer representing Kyoto Animation, &l;/span&g;&l;a href=\&q;https://twitter.com/DaisukeP/status/1154565063723773952\&q; target=\&q;_blank\&q;&g;&l;span style=\&q;font-weight: 400\&q;&g;tweeted&l;/span&g;&l;/a&g;&l;span style=\&q;font-weight: 400\&q;&g; that within 48 hours of posting the direct deposit information to donate to the studio&a;rsquo;s bank account, &l;/span&g;&l;a href=\&q;https://twitter.com/DaisukeP/status/1154565063723773952\&q; target=\&q;_blank\&q;&g;&l;span style=\&q;font-weight: 400\&q;&g;it had raised 401,255,554 yen&l;/span&g;&l;/a&g; or about $3,693,176.\r\n\r\nMeanwhile, Sentai Filmworks, which posted its GoFundMe the night of the fire, has &l;a href=\&q;https://www.gofundme.com/f/help-kyoani-heal\&q; target=\&q;_blank\&q;&g;raised more than $2 million&l;/a&g; for the studio. In response to fans&a;rsquo; questions, the company &l;a href=\&q;https://twitter.com/SentaiFilmworks/status/1154393937098039297\&q; target=\&q;_blank\&q;&g;released a statement Thursday&l;/a&g; that it is &a;ldquo;working with KyoAni&a;rsquo;s appointed representative&a;rdquo; to ensure the funds &a;ldquo;reach the KyoAni victims and their families in a direct and meaningful way.&a;rdquo;\r\n\r\nOther organizations, including a collaboration between Yahoo! Japan and JAniCA (Japanese Animation Creators Association), are also collecting funds for the victims. As of Friday, July 26, this fundraiser &l;a href=\&q;https://donation.yahoo.co.jp/detail/5234001/\&q; target=\&q;_blank\&q;&g;has netted 3,409,930 yen&l;/a&g; or about $31,381.59.\r\n\r\nRight now, the most straightforward way for fans to send monetary support to Kyoto Animation is to send a direct donation using the &l;a href=\&q;http://www.kyotoanimation.co.jp/information/?id=3075\&q; target=\&q;_blank\&q;&g;bank information the company has released itself&l;/a&g;, including a SWIFT code for international transfers. The bank account holder is Hideaki Hatta, the president of Kyoto Animation.\r\n\r\nThe information for donating is listed below.\r\n\r\nBANK NAME : THE KYOTO SHINKIN BANK\r\n\r\nSWIFT : KYSBJPJZ\r\n\r\nBRANCH NAME : MINAMI MOMOYAMA BRANCH\r\n\r\nBRANCH NUMBER : 048\r\n\r\nADDRESS : 16-50, YOSAI, MOMOYAMA-CHO, HUSHIMI-KU, KYOTO-SHI, KYOTO-HU, 612-8016 , JAPAN\r\n\r\nACCOUNT NUMBER : 0002890\r\n\r\nACCOUNT HOLDER : KYOTO ANIMATION CO.,LTD., REPRESENTATIVE DIRECTOR, HATTA HIDEAKI&l;/p&g;&q;,&q;description&q;:&q;Animators are beginning to rebuild Kyoto Animation. \n&l;p&g; \n &l;fbs-ad position=\&q;inread\&q; progressive=\&q;\&q;&g;&l;/fbs-ad&g;&l;/p&g; \n&l;p&g;Located in Uji, Kyoto Prefecture, Japan, Kyoto Animation established itself as a pillar of the animation industry with beloved titles like international hit movie &l;i&g;A Silent Voice&l;/i&g; and instant fan classics like &l;i&g;&l;span style=\&q;font-weight: 400\&q;&g;K-On!&l;/span&g;&l;/i&g;&l;span style=\&q;font-weight: 400\&q;&g;, &l;/span&g;&l;i&g;&l;span style=\&q;font-weight: 400\&q;&g;Free! Iwatobi Swim Club&l;/span&g;&l;/i&g;&l;span style=\&q;font-weight: 400\&q;&g;, and &l;/span&g;&l;i&g;&l;span style=\&q;font-weight: 400\&q;&g;The Melancholy of Haruhi Suzumiya&l;/span&g;&l;/i&g;&l;span style=\&q;font-weight: 400\&q;&g;. It differentiates itself from most other anime studios by &l;/span&g;&l;a href=\&q;https://www.forbes.com/sites/laurenorsini/2019/07/19/the-impact-of-kyoto-animation-5-things-you-need-to-know/#1687d14460d6\&q; target=\&q;_self\&q; data-ga-track=\&q;InternalLink:https://www.forbes.com/sites/laurenorsini/2019/07/19/the-impact-of-kyoto-animation-5-things-you-need-to-know/#1687d14460d6\&q;&g;&l;span style=\&q;font-weight: 400\&q; data-ga-track=\&q;InternalLink:https://www.forbes.com/sites/laurenorsini/2019/07/19/the-impact-of-kyoto-animation-5-things-you-need-to-know/#1687d14460d6\&q;&g;hiring animators as salaried employees&l;/span&g;&l;/a&g;, rather than contractors paid by the frame, so animators can focus on quality over quantity.&l;/p&g; \n&l;p&g;On July 18, one of the Kyoto Animation buildings was the target of a suspected arson attack that claimed 34 lives, including those of 13 men and 21 women. Thirty-four additional victims were injured. Most of the victims were &l;a href=\&q;https://www.theguardian.com/world/2019/jul/20/kyoto-animation-studio-fire-victims-mostly-in-their-20s-and-30s\&q; target=\&q;_blank\&q; rel=\&q;nofollow noopener\&q; data-ga-track=\&q;ExternalLink:https://www.theguardian.com/world/2019/jul/20/kyoto-animation-studio-fire-victims-mostly-in-their-20s-and-30s\&q;&g;in their 20s and 30s&l;/a&g;.&l;/p&g; \n&l;div class=\&q;vestpocket\&q; vest-pocket=\&q;\&q;&g;&l;/div&g; \n&l;p&g;&l;b&g;See also: &l;/b&g;&l;a href=\&q;https://www.forbes.com/sites/olliebarder/2019/07/18/kyoto-animation-fire-claims-33-lives-and-leaves-a-nation-in-shock/#3a8fbd1580ac\&q; target=\&q;_self\&q; data-ga-track=\&q;InternalLink:https://www.forbes.com/sites/olliebarder/2019/07/18/kyoto-animation-fire-claims-33-lives-and-leaves-a-nation-in-shock/#3a8fbd1580ac\&q;&g;&l;b data-ga-track=\&q;InternalLink:https://www.forbes.com/sites/olliebarder/2019/07/18/kyoto-animation-fire-claims-33-lives-and-leaves-a-nation-in-shock/#3a8fbd1580ac\&q;&g;Kyoto Animation Fire Claims 33 Lives And Leaves A Nation In Shock&l;/b&g;&l;/a&g;&l;/p&g; \n&l;p&g;Now, surviving animators, including some who &l;a href=\&q;https://www.crunchyroll.com/anime-news/2019/07/26/kyoto-animation-survivors-from-studio-1-return-to-work?utm_source=community_cr&a;amp;utm_medium=twitter&a;amp;utm_campaign=news&a;amp;referrer=community_cr_twitter_news\&q; target=\&q;_blank\&q; rel=\&q;nofollow noopener\&q; data-ga-track=\&q;ExternalLink:https://www.crunchyroll.com/anime-news/2019/07/26/kyoto-animation-survivors-from-studio-1-return-to-work?utm_source=community_cr&a;amp;utm_medium=twitter&a;amp;utm_campaign=news&a;amp;referrer=community_cr_twitter_news\&q;&g;&l;span style=\&q;font-weight: 400\&q; data-ga-track=\&q;ExternalLink:https://www.crunchyroll.com/anime-news/2019/07/26/kyoto-animation-survivors-from-studio-1-return-to-work?utm_source=community_cr&a;amp;utm_medium=twitter&a;amp;utm_campaign=news&a;amp;referrer=community_cr_twitter_news\&q;&g;dove out of second-story windows&l;/span&g;&l;/a&g;&l;span style=\&q;font-weight: 400\&q;&g; to escape the flames, are &l;/span&g;&l;a href=\&q;https://www.ktv.jp/news/articles/94cbcbe4952142f988acbec47e0f3391.html\&q; target=\&q;_blank\&q; rel=\&q;nofollow noopener\&q; data-ga-track=\&q;ExternalLink:https://www.ktv.jp/news/articles/94cbcbe4952142f988acbec47e0f3391.html\&q;&g;&l;span style=\&q;font-weight: 400\&q; data-ga-track=\&q;ExternalLink:https://www.ktv.jp/news/articles/94cbcbe4952142f988acbec47e0f3391.html\&q;&g;returning to work&l;/span&g;&l;/a&g;&l;span style=\&q;font-weight: 400\&q;&g; to attempt the uphill climb of rebuilding the studio’s legacy. But thanks to monetary support, KyoAni, as the studio is called by fans, won’t be doing it alone.&a;nbsp;&l;/span&g;&l;/p&g; \n&l;p&g;&l;span style=\&q;font-weight: 400\&q;&g;Daisuke Okeda, the lawyer representing Kyoto Animation, &l;/span&g;&l;a href=\&q;https://twitter.com/DaisukeP/status/1154565063723773952\&q; target=\&q;_blank\&q; rel=\&q;nofollow noopener\&q; data-ga-track=\&q;ExternalLink:https://twitter.com/DaisukeP/status/1154565063723773952\&q;&g;&l;span style=\&q;font-weight: 400\&q; data-ga-track=\&q;ExternalLink:https://twitter.com/DaisukeP/status/1154565063723773952\&q;&g;tweeted&l;/span&g;&l;/a&g;&l;span style=\&q;font-weight: 400\&q;&g; that within 48 hours of posting the direct deposit information to donate to the studio’s bank account, &l;/span&g;&l;a href=\&q;https://twitter.com/DaisukeP/status/1154565063723773952\&q; target=\&q;_blank\&q; rel=\&q;nofollow noopener\&q; data-ga-track=\&q;ExternalLink:https://twitter.com/DaisukeP/status/1154565063723773952\&q;&g;&l;span style=\&q;font-weight: 400\&q; data-ga-track=\&q;ExternalLink:https://twitter.com/DaisukeP/status/1154565063723773952\&q;&g;it had raised 401,255,554 yen&l;/span&g;&l;/a&g; or about $3,693,176.&l;/p&g; \n&l;p&g;Meanwhile, Sentai Filmworks, which posted its GoFundMe the night of the fire, has &l;a href=\&q;https://www.gofundme.com/f/help-kyoani-heal\&q; target=\&q;_blank\&q; rel=\&q;nofollow noopener\&q; data-ga-track=\&q;ExternalLink:https://www.gofundme.com/f/help-kyoani-heal\&q;&g;raised more than $2 million&l;/a&g; for the studio. In response to fans’ questions, the company &l;a href=\&q;https://twitter.com/SentaiFilmworks/status/1154393937098039297\&q; target=\&q;_blank\&q; rel=\&q;nofollow noopener\&q; data-ga-track=\&q;ExternalLink:https://twitter.com/SentaiFilmworks/status/1154393937098039297\&q;&g;released a statement Thursday&l;/a&g; that it is “working with KyoAni’s appointed representative” to ensure the funds “reach the KyoAni victims and their families in a direct and meaningful way.”&l;/p&g; \n&l;p&g;Other organizations, including a collaboration between Yahoo! Japan and JAniCA (Japanese Animation Creators Association), are also collecting funds for the victims. As of Friday, July 26, this fundraiser &l;a href=\&q;https://donation.yahoo.co.jp/detail/5234001/\&q; target=\&q;_blank\&q; rel=\&q;nofollow noopener\&q; data-ga-track=\&q;ExternalLink:https://donation.yahoo.co.jp/detail/5234001/\&q;&g;has netted 3,409,930 yen&l;/a&g; or about $31,381.59.&l;/p&g; \n&l;p&g;Right now, the most straightforward way for fans to send monetary support to Kyoto Animation is to send a direct donation using the &l;a href=\&q;http://www.kyotoanimation.co.jp/information/?id=3075\&q; target=\&q;_blank\&q; rel=\&q;nofollow noopener\&q; data-ga-track=\&q;ExternalLink:http://www.kyotoanimation.co.jp/information/?id=3075\&q;&g;bank information the company has released itself&l;/a&g;, including a SWIFT code for international transfers. The bank account holder is Hideaki Hatta, the president of Kyoto Animation.&l;/p&g; \n&l;p&g;The information for donating is listed below.&l;/p&g; \n&l;p&g;BANK NAME : THE KYOTO SHINKIN BANK&l;/p&g;
